This application will track all of your encrypted files/folders and allow you to reference those keys if need be, if you forget what you used as a pass phrase.\r\n\r\nThe only way you can access those keys though is you have to know the Master Key that you use to encrypt the whole data set.  But, you can also share encrypted files with friends as long as they have TNO Crypt and know the private key / password you assigned to the file.  With these two things then they can decrypt it on their end.  It is extremely secure, implementing AES 256 encryption as well as SALT and HASH of the information on top of that.\r\n\r\nIt also supports FULL steganography, meaning you can hide both an image within an image as well as a large amount of text.
